    "text": "No, they're not longitudinal right now. Here's the current flow:\n\n**What exists:**\n- Interview (AI chat) \u2192 Exam (click systems) \u2192 Labs (order \u2192 delay \u2192 results) \u2192 Imaging (order \u2192 delay \u2192 results) \u2192 Disposition (discharge/admit/transfer) \u2192 Teaching debrief\n\n**What's missing for longitudinal care:**\n- No **treatment ordering** (meds, IV fluids, procedures like intubation or chest tube)\n- No **reassessment** \u2014 vitals don't change after interventions, patient status doesn't evolve\n- No **time progression** \u2014 labs come back in 3-6 seconds, not real-time simulation\n- No **response to treatment** \u2014 can't give calcium gluconate for hyperkalemia and see the ECG normalize, can't give tPA and reassess neuro exam\n\nSo right now it's a single-pass diagnostic exercise: gather info \u2192 make a disposition. The teaching section covers what treatments *should* be ordered, but the student never actually does it.\n\nWould you want to build out a treatment/reassessment layer? The architecture could support something like: after labs/imaging result, a **Treatment** tab unlocks where students order interventions from a standardized menu, then a **Reassess** option shows updated vitals and exam findings based on whether they picked the right treatments. Each case template would need a `treatments` object with correct/incorrect options and corresponding reassessment states.\n\nWant me to scope that out or is that a future phase?",
    "citations": []
  }
]
